60	def _build_model(modality_info: dict, model_name: str):
61	    """Encoder embeddings for all inputs; decoder embeddings only for vision targets."""
62	    from fourm.utils import create_model
63	
64	    def _instantiate(mod: str, key: str):
65	        info = modality_info[mod]
66	        is_img = info["type"] == "img"
67	        kw = dict(patch_size=info.get("patch_size", 16), image_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
68	        return info[key](**(kw if is_img else {}))
69	
70	    enc = {mod: _instantiate(mod, "encoder_embedding") for mod in _IN_DOMAINS}
71	    dec = {mod: _instantiate(mod, "decoder_embedding") for mod in _OUT_DOMAINS}
72	    return create_model(
73	        model_name, encoder_embeddings=enc, decoder_embeddings=dec,
74	        modality_info=modality_info, num_register_tokens=0,
75	    )
76	
77	
78	def _fixed_batch(batch_size: int, input_tokens: int, target_tokens: int, seed: int):
79	    """Build one collated batch; retry seeds until every modality has targets."""
80	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
81	    from fourm.data.modality_transforms import IdentityTransform, UnifiedDataTransform
82	    from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import setup_sampling_mod_info
83	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import default_collate
84	    from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
85	    from things_augmenter import ThingsImageAugmenter
86	    from train_4m import _build_modality_info
87	
88	    ds_cfg = {
89	        "in_domains": "-".join(sorted(_IN_DOMAINS)),
90	        "out_domains": "-".join(sorted(_OUT_DOMAINS)),
91	        "input_alphas": "-".join("1.0" for _ in _IN_DOMAINS),
92	        "target_alphas": "-".join("1.0" for _ in _OUT_DOMAINS),
93	    }
94	    from tokenizers import Tokenizer
95	
96	    text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(str(TEXT_TOKENIZER))
97	    full = _build_modality_info(_IN_DOMAINS, input_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
98	    mask_info, _ = setup_sampling_mod_info(ds_cfg, full)
99	
100	    transforms = dict(MODALITY_TRANSFORMS)
101	    transforms["__key__"] = IdentityTransform()
102	    udt = UnifiedDataTransform(
103	        transforms_dict=transforms,
104	        image_augmenter=ThingsImageAugmenter(
105	            target_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE, no_aug=True, main_domain="tok_rgb"
106	        ),
107	    )
108	
109	    for attempt in range(seed, seed + 50):
110	        torch.manual_seed(attempt)
111	        masker = PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
112	            modality_info=mask_info, text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
113	            input_tokens_range=(input_tokens, input_tokens),
114	            target_tokens_range=(target_tokens, target_tokens),
115	        )
116	        rng = np.random.default_rng(attempt)
117	        samples = [masker(udt(_decoded_sample(rng))) for _ in range(batch_size)]
118	        batch = default_collate(samples)
119	        targets = {m: int((~batch[m]["target_mask"]).sum()) for m in _OUT_DOMAINS}
120	        if all(v > 0 for v in targets.values()):
121	            return batch, full, mask_info, targets
122	    raise RuntimeError(f"could not build a batch with targets for all out-domains: {targets}")
123	
124	
125	def run_overfit(
126	    steps: int = 150,
127	    batch_size: int = 2,
128	    input_tokens: int = 48,
129	    target_tokens: int = 48,
130	    lr: float = 2e-3,
131	    model_name: str = "fm_tiny_6e_6d_swiglu_nobias",
132	    seed: int = 0,
133	    device: str | None = None,
134	    log_every: int = 25,
135	) -> dict[str, list[float]]:
136	    """Run ``steps`` optimizer steps on one fixed batch; return per-modality loss history.
137	
138	    A small target budget on a tiny batch lets ``fm_tiny`` drive every modality's
139	    loss toward zero. ``model.eval()`` disables dropout so the descent is clean and
140	    the run is deterministic (the only per-step variation, 4M's modality shuffle, is
141	    loss-invariant); we still optimize all parameters.
142	    """
143	    device = torch.device(device or ("cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu"))
144	    batch, model_info, _, targets = _fixed_batch(batch_size, input_tokens, target_tokens, seed)

=== modal driver ===
"""Bridge between Modal scripts and modal_image.py.

Why this exists:
  - On your laptop, modal_image.py sits next to this file.
  - In the Modal container, the repo is mounted at /opt/repo/4m_training/.
  This loader tries both locations so every modal_*.py can share one image file.

You usually don't need to edit this — copy it verbatim into new training folders.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import importlib.util
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from types import ModuleType


def load_modal_image() -> ModuleType:
    """Import modal_image.py and return it as a module."""
    # Reuse if already loaded (e.g. multiple modal scripts in one process).
    if "modal_image" in sys.modules:
        return sys.modules["modal_image"]

    # Try container path first, then local path next to this file.
    for path in (
        Path("/opt/repo/4m_training/modal/modal_image.py"),
        Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "modal_image.py",
    ):
        if not path.is_file():
            continue
        spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("modal_image", path)
        if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
            continue
        mod = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
        sys.modules["modal_image"] = mod
        spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
        return mod

    raise ImportError(
        "modal_image.py not found under /opt/repo/4m_training (repo mount missing?)"
    )

3	The Modal ``prod_things`` smoke hit ``scatter gather kernel index out of bounds`` on the

6	  H1 — Text sentinel leakage (primary):
7	      ``tok_meg`` / ``tok_eeg`` are ``seq_token`` but stock ``sequence_token_mask`` injects
8	      text-tokenizer sentinel ids (often >30k) into tensors fed to small-vocab embeddings.

=== _build_modality_info from committed 7bd68b7 ===
def _build_modality_info(
    all_domain_names: list[str],
    input_size: int = THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
) -> dict:
    import copy

    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO

    # Model + masking only need in/out token domains, not presence flags.
    token_domains = [d for d in all_domain_names if not d.endswith("_mask")]
    modality_info = {
        mod: copy.deepcopy(MODALITY_INFO[mod])
        for mod in token_domains
        if mod in MODALITY_INFO
    }
    for mod, info in modality_info.items():
        if info.get("type") == "img":
            patch_size = info.get("patch_size", THINGS_PATCH_SIZE)
            info["max_tokens"] = pretoken_grid_num_tokens(input_size, patch_size)
    return modality_info


def _iterate_loader(loader, n_batches: int, label: str) -> None:
    print(f"{label}: iterating {n_batches} batches…\n")
    for i, batch in enumerate(loader):
        if i >= n_batches:
            break
        print(f"batch {i}: keys = {sorted(batch.keys())}")
        for k, v in batch.items():
            if isinstance(v, dict) and "tensor" in v:
                print(f"  {k:>16s} : tensor shape={tuple(v['tensor'].shape)}")
            else:
                shape = getattr(v, "shape", None)
                print(
                    f"  {k:>16s} : shape={tuple(shape) if shape is not None else type(v).__name__}"
                )
        print()


# Stock mixture loader computes epoch_size // (num_gpus * num_workers * batch_size),
# so the dryrun cannot use 0 workers. One worker keeps it cheap and single-process.
_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS = 1


def run_dryrun(config_path: Path, n_batches: int = 4) -> None:
    modality_info_full = _build_modality_info(all_domains, input_size)
    mod_info, sampling_weights = setup_sampling_mod_info(train_ds, modality_info_full)

    tok_path = main_cfg.get(
        "text_tokenizer_path",
        str(_REPO_ROOT / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"),
    )
    text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(tok_path)

    train_loader = get_train_dataloader(
        dataset_config=train_ds,
        modality_info=mod_info,
        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
        input_size=input_size,
        num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
        num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
        min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
        min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
        num_tasks=1,
        num_workers=_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS,
        dataset_batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
        epoch_size=main_cfg.get("epoch_size", max(n_batches * 4, 16)),
    )
    _iterate_loader(train_loader, n_batches, "train dryrun")

    if val_ds.get("data_path"):
        val_loader = get_val_dataloader(
            dataset_config=val_ds,
            dataset_name="things",
            train_configs={"things": train_ds},
            modality_info=mod_info,
            sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
            text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
            input_size=input_size,

Assistant2026-05-27T19:54:14.339Z

I've now mapped the system end to end. Before writing code, two things — one blocker I have to correct, and the core design decision I need you to make.

1. train_4m.py is not in lib/ — its source is actually gone

I checked carefully. There is no train_4m.py anywhere live in the tree (not in 4m_training/, not in lib/, not under .venv). What exists:

  • A stale compiled artifact: 4m_training/__pycache__/train_4m.cpython-313.pyc
  • A committed copy on the add_4m branch: 7bd68b7:4m_training/train_4m.py (old layout, predates the current modal/ reorg)

This matters because validate_4m.py, overfit_smoke.py, and three test files all do from train_4m import _build_modality_info — so the test suite and validation runner are currently import-broken. _build_modality_info is also exactly the function that sets max_tokens for img modalities, which this feature has to touch. So I need a real train_4m.py before I can test anything.

Recovery options: (a) restore from commit 7bd68b7 and reconcile to the current layout, or (b) decompile the .pyc (Python 3.13, harder), or (c) you point me to where it really lives if my search missed it.

2. The core design decision: how MEG becomes a target

Your own design note (notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md §6) already anticipated this and the code confirms the constraints:

  • The type must change from seq_token to img. In fm.py:309, seq_token targets go through an autoregressive left-shift path that silently drops the scattered targets your image_mask masking produces — the documented "MEG loss = 0" bug. img type uses the parallel mask-token branch (fm.py:320), which is what you want. Bonus: this lets me delete the _NEURAL_FLAT_TOKEN_MODS hack in neural_masking.py.
  • The loss is one cross-entropy per modality, single head (fm.py:597). EEG fits this directly (flat 17, one 8192-vocab head). MEG is the problem: each of 128 cells carries 4 RVQ codes with layer-specific 512-vocab codebooks. One head can't predict 4 codes, and I will not modify external/ml-4m.

EEG is unambiguous — one img modality, 17 positions, vocab 8192. For MEG, here are the three faithful-to-the-constraint options:

AST-based import resolution audit
python3 - <<'PY'
import ast, pathlib, sys
root = pathlib.Path('.')
# Build set of local module names available on the import path (lib/, root, modal/)
search_dirs = [root/'lib', root, root/'modal']
local_mods = set()
for d in search_dirs:
    if d.is_dir():
        for p in d.glob('*.py'):
            local_mods.add(p.stem)
stdlib_third = set('''fourm torch numpy os sys io copy json math random functools pathlib typing
argparse tarfile importlib types collections dataclasses itertools warnings subprocess time re
tokenizers einops PIL webdataset yaml pytest wandb modal abc contextlib enum shutil tempfile glob
datetime logging __future__ pickle hashlib unittest gzip struct'''.split())

imported = {}
for p in root.rglob('*.py'):
    if '__pycache__' in p.parts: continue
    try:
        tree = ast.parse(p.read_text())
    except Exception as e:
        print("PARSE-ERR", p, e); continue
    for node in ast.walk(tree):
        if isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom) and node.level==0 and node.module:
            top = node.module.split('.')[0]
            imported.setdefault(top, set()).add(str(p))
        elif isinstance(node, ast.Import):
            for n in node.names:
                top = n.name.split('.')[0]
                imported.setdefault(top, set()).add(str(p))

missing = {}
for mod, where in sorted(imported.items()):
    if mod in stdlib_third: continue
    if mod in local_mods: continue
    # not resolvable as a local module
    missing[mod] = where

if not missing:
    print("All local imports resolve. No missing modules.")
else:
    print("UNRESOLVED local imports:")
    for mod, where in missing.items():
        print(f"  {mod}  <- imported by:")
        for w in sorted(where): print(f"      {w}")
print()
print("Local modules found:", ', '.join(sorted(local_mods)))

45	def _make_tar(path: Path, entries: list[tuple[str, str, bytes]]) -> None:
46	    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
47	    with tarfile.open(path, "w") as tar:
48	        for key, ext, data in entries:
49	            info = tarfile.TarInfo(name=f"{key}.{ext}")
50	            info.size = len(data)
51	            tar.addfile(info, io.BytesIO(data))

54	def _npy_bytes(arr: np.ndarray) -> bytes:
55	    buf = io.BytesIO()
56	    np.save(buf, arr, allow_pickle=False)
57	    return buf.getvalue()
58	
59	
60	def run_demo() -> None:
61	    """Build a synthetic shard and walk samples through the 4M decode path."""
62	    import webdataset as wds
63	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
64	        filter_metadata,
65	        multi_tarfile_samples,
66	        remove_extensions,
67	        tok_to_int64,
68	        wds_decoder,
69	    )
70	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import map as keyless_map
71	
72	    from fourm_neural_transforms import EegTokTransform, MegTokTransform
73	
74	    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:
75	        root = Path(tmp) / "things"
76	        ids = ["000000001", "000000002", "000000003"]
77	
78	        rgb_arr = lambda i: np.full((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), int(i), dtype=np.int16)
79	        depth_arr = np.zeros((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), dtype=np.int16)
80	        meg_real = np.full((4, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 7, dtype=np.int16)
81	        meg_sentinel = np.full((1, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
82	        eeg_real = np.full((2, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 3, dtype=np.int16)
83	        eeg_sentinel = np.full((1, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
84	        mask_real = np.array([1], dtype=np.uint8)
85	        mask_zero = np.array([0], dtype=np.uint8)
86	
87	        for mod, arrs in [
88	            ("tok_rgb", [(i, _npy_bytes(rgb_arr(i))) for i in ids]),
89	            ("tok_depth", [(i, _npy_bytes(depth_arr)) for i in ids]),
90	            (
91	                "tok_meg",
92	                [
93	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
94	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(meg_sentinel)),
95	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
96	                ],
97	            ),
98	            (
99	                "tok_eeg",
100	                [
101	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
102	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(eeg_sentinel)),
103	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
104	                ],
105	            ),
106	            (
107	                "meg_mask",
108	                [
109	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
110	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
111	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
112	                ],
113	            ),
114	            (
115	                "eeg_mask",
116	                [
117	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
118	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
119	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
120	                ],
121	            ),
122	        ]:
123	            _make_tar(
124	                root / f"{mod}/shard_000.tar",
125	                [(k, "npy", b) for k, b in arrs],
126	            )
127	
128	        url = (
129	            f"{root}/[tok_rgb,tok_depth,tok_meg,tok_eeg,meg_mask,eeg_mask]/"
130	            "shard_000.tar"
131	        )
132	        print(f"data_path = {url}\n")
133	
134	        pipeline = wds.DataPipeline(
135	            wds.SimpleShardList(url),
136	            partial(multi_tarfile_samples, handler=lambda e: (_ for _ in ()).throw(e)),
137	            wds.decode(wds_decoder),
138	            wds.map(remove_extensions),
139	            keyless_map(filter_metadata),
140	            keyless_map(tok_to_int64),
141	        )
142	
143	        print("=" * 72)
144	        print("  4M pipeline output (after decode + filter)")
145	        print("=" * 72)
146	        for sample in pipeline:
147	            shapes = {
148	                k: getattr(v, "shape", type(v).__name__) for k, v in sample.items()
149	            }
150	            print(f"  modalities = {sorted(sample)}")
151	            print(f"  shapes     = {shapes}")
152	            print()
153	
154	        print("=" * 72)
155	        print("  After trial transforms")
156	        print("=" * 72)
157	        meg_tx = MegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
158	        eeg_tx = EegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
159	        for label, arr, tx in [
160	            ("MEG real", meg_real, meg_tx),
161	            ("MEG sentinel", meg_sentinel, meg_tx),
162	            ("EEG real", eeg_real, eeg_tx),
163	            ("EEG sentinel", eeg_sentinel, eeg_tx),
164	        ]:
165	            tokens = tx.preprocess(arr)
166	            print(f"  {label:>14s}: in={tuple(arr.shape)} -> out={tuple(tokens.shape)}")
167

169	def _load_configs(config_path: Path) -> tuple[dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any]]:
170	    """Return (main_cfg, train_ds_cfg, val_ds_cfg_or_empty). Accepts main or data yaml."""
171	    import yaml
172	
173	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
174	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
175	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
176	
177	    with open(config_path) as f:
178	        cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
179	
180	    if "train" in cfg and "datasets" in cfg.get("train", {}):
181	        main = {
182	            "input_size": THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
183	            "num_input_tokens": 256,
184	            "num_target_tokens": 256,
185	            "batch_size": 4,
186	            "epoch_size": 64,
187	            "text_tokenizer_path": str(
188	                _REPO_ROOT
189	                / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"
190	            ),
191	        }
192	        train_ds = next(iter(cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
193	        val_ds = {}
194	        if "val" in cfg and cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
195	            val_ds = next(iter(cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
196	        return main, train_ds, val_ds
197	
198	    data_rel = cfg.get("data_config")
199	    if not data_rel:
200	        raise ValueError(f"{config_path}: expected data_config or train.datasets")
201	    data_path = Path(data_rel)
202	    if not data_path.is_absolute():
203	        data_path = (_REPO_ROOT / data_path).resolve()
204	    with open(data_path) as f:
205	        data_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
206	    train_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
207	    val_ds = {}
208	    if "val" in data_cfg and data_cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
209	        val_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
210	    return cfg, train_ds, val_ds
211	
212	
213	def run_validate(config_path: Path) -> None:
214	    from config_validate import validate_config_file
215	
216	    errors = validate_config_file(config_path, _REPO_ROOT)
217	    if errors:
218	        print(f"FAIL {config_path}:")
219	        for e in errors:
220	            print(f"  - {e}")
221	        raise SystemExit(1)
222	    print(f"OK {config_path}")

225	def _build_modality_info(
226	    all_domain_names: list[str],
227	    input_size: int = THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
228	) -> dict:
229	    import copy
230	
231	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
232	
233	    # Model + masking only need in/out token domains, not presence flags.
234	    token_domains = [d for d in all_domain_names if not d.endswith("_mask")]
235	    modality_info = {
236	        mod: copy.deepcopy(MODALITY_INFO[mod])
237	        for mod in token_domains
238	        if mod in MODALITY_INFO
239	    }
240	    for mod, info in modality_info.items():
241	        if info.get("type") == "img":
242	            patch_size = info.get("patch_size", THINGS_PATCH_SIZE)
243	            info["max_tokens"] = pretoken_grid_num_tokens(input_size, patch_size)
244	    return modality_info
245	
246	
247	def _iterate_loader(loader, n_batches: int, label: str) -> None:
248	    print(f"{label}: iterating {n_batches} batches…\n")
249	    for i, batch in enumerate(loader):
250	        if i >= n_batches:
251	            break
252	        print(f"batch {i}: keys = {sorted(batch.keys())}")
253	        for k, v in batch.items():
254	            if isinstance(v, dict) and "tensor" in v:
255	                print(f"  {k:>16s} : tensor shape={tuple(v['tensor'].shape)}")
256	            else:
257	                shape = getattr(v, "shape", None)
258	                print(
259	                    f"  {k:>16s} : shape={tuple(shape) if shape is not None else type(v).__name__}"
260	                )
261	        print()
262	
263	
264	# Stock mixture loader computes epoch_size // (num_gpus * num_workers * batch_size),
265	# so the dryrun cannot use 0 workers. One worker keeps it cheap and single-process.
266	_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS = 1
267	
268	
269	def run_dryrun(config_path: Path, n_batches: int = 4) -> None:
270	    """Build train + val dataloaders and iterate a few batches."""
271	    from tokenizers import Tokenizer
272	
273	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
274	    from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import get_train_dataloader, get_val_dataloader, setup_sampling_mod_info
275	
276	    main_cfg, train_ds, val_ds = _load_configs(config_path)
277	    input_size = main_cfg.get("input_size", THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
278	
279	    in_domains = sorted(train_ds["in_domains"].split("-"))
280	    out_domains = sorted(train_ds["out_domains"].split("-"))
281	    all_domains = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
282	    modality_info_full = _build_modality_info(all_domains, input_size)
283	    mod_info, sampling_weights = setup_sampling_mod_info(train_ds, modality_info_full)
284	
285	    tok_path = main_cfg.get(
286	        "text_tokenizer_path",
287	        str(_REPO_ROOT / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"),
288	    )
289	    text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(tok_path)
290	
291	    train_loader = get_train_dataloader(
292	        dataset_config=train_ds,
293	        modality_info=mod_info,
294	        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
295	        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
296	        input_size=input_size,
297	        num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
298	        num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
299	        min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
300	        min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
301	        num_tasks=1,
302	        num_workers=_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS,
303	        dataset_batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
304	        epoch_size=main_cfg.get("epoch_size", max(n_batches * 4, 16)),
305	    )
306	    _iterate_loader(train_loader, n_batches, "train dryrun")
307	
308	    if val_ds.get("data_path"):
309	        val_loader = get_val_dataloader(
310	            dataset_config=val_ds,
311	            dataset_name="things",
312	            train_configs={"things": train_ds},
313	            modality_info=mod_info,
314	            sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
315	            text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
316	            input_size=input_size,
317	            num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
318	            num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
319	            min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
320	            min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
321	            fixed_eval=False,
322	            fixed_eval_input_tokens=128,
323	            fixed_eval_target_tokens=128,
324	            dist_eval=False,
325	            num_tasks=1,
326	            num_workers=0,
327	            batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
328	            pin_mem=False,
329	        )
330	        _iterate_loader(val_loader, n_batches, "val dryrun")
331	
332	
333	def _clean_extra_argv(extra_argv: list[str]) -> list[str]:
334	    """Drop the leading ``--`` separator argparse.REMAINDER keeps.
335	
336	    ``train --config X -- --data_config Y`` captures ``['--', '--data_config', Y]``.
337	    The 4M trainer's argparse treats a forwarded ``--`` as a positional and errors
338	    ("unrecognized arguments"), so strip exactly the one leading separator.
339	    """
340	    if extra_argv and extra_argv[0] == "--":
341	        return extra_argv[1:]
342	    return extra_argv
343	
344	
345	def run_train(config_path: Path, extra_argv: list[str]) -> None:
346	    """Hand off to 4M's official trainer with neural patches active."""
347	    import os
348	    import runpy
349	
350	    extra_argv = _clean_extra_argv(extra_argv)
351	
352	    # Stock run_training_4m.py always uses DDP; set single-process vars if missing.
353	    os.environ.setdefault("RANK", "0")
354	    os.environ.setdefault("WORLD_SIZE", "1")
355	    os.environ.setdefault("LOCAL_RANK", "0")
356	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_ADDR", "127.0.0.1")
357	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_PORT", "29500")
358	
359	    ml_4m_root = _REPO_ROOT / "external" / "ml-4m"
360	    if not (ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py").exists():
361	        raise FileNotFoundError(
362	            f"4M trainer not found at {ml_4m_root}. "
363	            "Install with: pip install -e external/ml-4m"
364	        )
365	    sys.path.insert(0, str(ml_4m_root))
366	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
367	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
368	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
369	
370	    sys.argv = ["run_training_4m.py", "-c", str(config_path), *extra_argv]
371	    print(f"handing off to 4M trainer: argv = {sys.argv}\n")
372	    try:
373	        runpy.run_path(str(ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py"), run_name="__main__")
374	    finally:
375	        # Stock trainer inits the process group but never tears it down; doing it
376	        # here avoids the "destroy_process_group() was not called" NCCL warning.
377	        import torch.distributed as dist
378	
379	        if dist.is_available() and dist.is_initialized():
380	            dist.destroy_process_group()
381	
382	
383	def main() -> None:
384	    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
385	        description=__doc__,
386	        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
387	    )
388	    sub = p.add_subparsers(dest="mode", required=True)
389	
390	    sub.add_parser("demo", help="Synthetic shard pipeline walkthrough.")
391	
392	    p_dry = sub.add_parser("dryrun", help="Iterate train + val batches from config.")
393	    p_dry.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
394	    p_dry.add_argument("--n-batches", type=int, default=4)
395	
396	    p_train = sub.add_parser("train", help="Run 4M run_training_4m.py.")
397	    p_train.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
398	    p_train.add_argument("extra", nargs=argparse.REMAINDER)
399	
400	    p_val = sub.add_parser("validate", help="Check main/data YAML against 4M (no GPU/data).")
401	    p_val.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
402	
403	    args = p.parse_args()
404	    if args.mode == "demo":
405	        run_demo()
406	    elif args.mode == "dryrun":
407	        run_dryrun(args.config, args.n_batches)
408	    elif args.mode == "validate":
409	        run_validate(args.config)
410	    elif args.mode == "train":
411	        run_train(args.config, args.extra or [])
412	
413	
414	if __name__ == "__main__":
415	    main()

Assistant2026-05-27T19:57:51.967Z

Critical integration detail at run_training_4m.py:242-253: the stock trainer overwrites max_tokens for every img-type modality with (image_size // patch_size)² — always a perfect square. Our neural grids are 128 (=16×8) and 17, neither of which is a perfect square. So a plain img type is structurally incompatible with the real trainer. Let me check every place ml-4m branches on modality type to find the safe path.

1	"""Validate 4M main + data YAML configs against stock 4M and our neural extensions."""
2	
3	from __future__ import annotations
4	
5	import re
6	from pathlib import Path
7	from typing import Any
8	
9	import braceexpand
10	import yaml
11	
12	from repo_paths import REPO_ROOT as _REPO_ROOT
13	
14	_PRESENCE_FLAGS = frozenset({"meg_mask", "eeg_mask"})
15	# Neural modalities are encoder-only here (no decoder embedding); see
16	# notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md. Listing them as targets would crash model build.
17	_INPUT_ONLY = frozenset({"tok_meg", "tok_eeg"})
18	_TRAIN_TYPES = frozenset({"multimodal"})
19	_LOSS_TYPES = frozenset({"mod", "token"})
20	
21	
22	def _resolve(repo_root: Path, path_str: str) -> Path:
23	    p = Path(path_str)
24	    return p if p.is_absolute() else (repo_root / p).resolve()
25	
26	
27	def _modalities_in_bracket(data_path: str) -> list[str]:
28	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import extract_modality_names
29	
30	    m = re.search(r"\[([^\]]+)\]", data_path)
31	    if not m:
32	        return []
33	    return extract_modality_names(f"{{{m.group(1)}}}")
34	
35	
36	def expand_shard_urls(data_path: str) -> list[str]:
37	    """Brace-expand a 4M ``data_path``; raises if pattern is invalid."""
38	    return list(braceexpand.braceexpand(data_path))
39	
40	
41	def _parse_alphas(value: Any, n_domains: int, label: str) -> None:
42	    if value is None:
43	        return
44	    if not isinstance(value, str):
45	        raise ValueError(f"{label} must be a string or null, got {type(value)}")
46	    parts = value.split("-")
47	    if len(parts) not in (1, n_domains):
48	        raise ValueError(
49	            f"{label} has {len(parts)} value(s) but expected 1 or {n_domains} "
50	            f"(domains hyphen-separated)"
51	        )
52	    for p in parts:
53	        float(p)
54	
55	
56	def validate_dataset_config(
57	    name: str,
58	    cfg: dict[str, Any],
59	    repo_root: Path,
60	    modality_info: dict,
61	) -> list[str]:
62	    """Return list of error strings (empty = ok)."""
63	    errors: list[str] = []
64	
65	    if cfg.get("type") not in _TRAIN_TYPES:
66	        errors.append(f"{name}: type must be 'multimodal', got {cfg.get('type')!r}")
67	
68	    data_path = cfg.get("data_path", "")
69	    if not data_path:
70	        errors.append(f"{name}: missing data_path")
71	        return errors
72	
73	    if cfg.get("use_wds", True):
74	        try:
75	            urls = expand_shard_urls(data_path)
76	        except Exception as e:
77	            errors.append(f"{name}: data_path braceexpand failed: {e}")
78	            return errors
79	
80	        if any("{" in u or "}" in u for u in urls):
81	            errors.append(
82	                f"{name}: data_path has unexpanded braces (use ranges like "
83	                f"shard_{{000..026}}.tar not shard_{{000}}.tar): {data_path}"
84	            )
85	        if not urls:
86	            errors.append(f"{name}: data_path expanded to zero shard URLs")
87	
88	    in_domains = sorted(cfg.get("in_domains", "").split("-"))
89	    out_domains = sorted(cfg.get("out_domains", "").split("-"))
90	    if not in_domains or not out_domains:
91	        errors.append(f"{name}: in_domains and out_domains are required")
92	        return errors
93	
94	    for dom in in_domains + out_domains:
95	        if dom in _PRESENCE_FLAGS:
96	            errors.append(
97	                f"{name}: {dom} is a presence flag — keep it in data_path "
98	                f"brackets only, not in_domains/out_domains"
99	            )
100	        elif dom not in modality_info:
101	            errors.append(f"{name}: unknown modality {dom!r} (not in MODALITY_INFO)")
102	
103	    for dom in out_domains:
104	        if dom in _INPUT_ONLY:
105	            errors.append(
106	                f"{name}: {dom} is input-only (no decoder embedding) — keep it in "
107	                f"in_domains, not out_domains. See notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md"
108	            )
109	
110	    bracket_mods = _modalities_in_bracket(data_path)
111	    train_domains = set(in_domains) | set(out_domains)
112	    for dom in train_domains:
113	        if dom not in bracket_mods and dom not in _PRESENCE_FLAGS:
114	            errors.append(
115	                f"{name}: {dom} in in/out_domains but not in data_path "
116	                f"bracket list {bracket_mods}"
117	            )
118	
119	    main_aug = cfg.get("main_augment_domain")
120	    if main_aug and main_aug not in modality_info:
121	        errors.append(f"{name}: main_augment_domain {main_aug!r} not in MODALITY_INFO")
122	
123	    try:
124	        _parse_alphas(cfg.get("input_alphas"), len(in_domains), f"{name}.input_alphas")
125	        _parse_alphas(cfg.get("target_alphas"), len(out_domains), f"{name}.target_alphas")
126	    except ValueError as e:
127	        errors.append(str(e))
128	
129	    alphas_cfg = cfg.get("alphas_config")
130	    if alphas_cfg:
131	        if not _resolve(repo_root, alphas_cfg).is_file():
132	            errors.append(f"{name}: alphas_config not found: {alphas_cfg}")
133	
134	    return errors
135	
136	
137	def validate_data_config(
138	    data_cfg: dict[str, Any],
139	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
140	) -> list[str]:
141	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
142	    import fourm_neural_modalities  # noqa: F401 — register aliases + neural mods
143	
144	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
145	
146	    errors: list[str] = []
147	    train = data_cfg.get("train", {})
148	    datasets = train.get("datasets", {})
149	    if not datasets:
150	        return ["train.datasets is empty"]
151	
152	    weights = train.get("weights", [1.0])
153	    if len(weights) != len(datasets):
154	        errors.append(
155	            f"train.weights length {len(weights)} != "
156	            f"number of datasets {len(datasets)}"
157	        )
158	
159	    for name, ds in datasets.items():
160	        errors.extend(validate_dataset_config(name, ds, repo_root, MODALITY_INFO))
161	
162	    return errors
163	
164	
165	def validate_main_config(
166	    main_cfg: dict[str, Any],
167	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
168	) -> list[str]:
169	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
170	    errors: list[str] = []
171	
172	    from fourm.models import fm
173	
174	    model = main_cfg.get("model", "")
175	    if model not in fm.__all__:
176	        errors.append(f"unknown model {model!r}; choose from fourm.models.fm.__all__")
177	
178	    if main_cfg.get("loss_type") not in _LOSS_TYPES:
179	        errors.append(f"loss_type must be one of {_LOSS_TYPES}")
180	
181	    tok_path = main_cfg.get("text_tokenizer_path", "")
182	    if tok_path and not _resolve(repo_root, tok_path).is_file():
183	        errors.append(f"text_tokenizer_path not found: {tok_path}")
184	
185	    num_workers = main_cfg.get("num_workers", 10)
186	    if num_workers is not None and int(num_workers) < 1:
187	        errors.append("num_workers must be >= 1 (stock mixture loader divides by it)")
188	
189	    batch_size = main_cfg.get("batch_size", 0)
190	    epoch_size = main_cfg.get("epoch_size", 0)
191	    if batch_size and epoch_size:
192	        steps = int(epoch_size) // (int(batch_size) * 1)
193	        if steps < 1:
194	            errors.append(
195	                f"epoch_size ({epoch_size}) // batch_size ({batch_size}) must be >= 1"
196	            )
197	
198	    data_config = main_cfg.get("data_config", "")
199	    if not data_config:
200	        errors.append("main config missing data_config")
201	        return errors
202	
203	    data_path = _resolve(repo_root, data_config)
204	    if not data_path.is_file():
205	        errors.append(f"data_config not found: {data_config}")
206	        return errors
207	
208	    with open(data_path) as f:
209	        data_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
210	    errors.extend(validate_data_config(data_cfg, repo_root))
211	    return errors
212	
213	
214	def load_yaml(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
215	    with open(path) as f:
216	        return yaml.safe_load(f)
217	
218	
219	def validate_config_file(
220	    config_path: Path | str,
221	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
222	) -> list[str]:
223	    """Validate a main yaml (has data_config) or a standalone data yaml."""
224	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
225	    path = _resolve(repo_root, str(config_path))
226	    cfg = load_yaml(path)
227	    if "train" in cfg and "datasets" in cfg.get("train", {}):
228	        return validate_data_config(cfg, repo_root)
229	    return validate_main_config(cfg, repo_root)

1	"""Minimal hooks so stock 4M dataloaders work with THINGS neural shards.
2	
3	We do **not** reimplement the WebDataset pipeline. Instead we patch three
4	integration points and delegate everything else to upstream 4M:
5	
6	  * ``UnifiedMasking`` → ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking`` (meg/eeg absence)
7	  * ``PreTokenizedImageAugmenter`` → ``ThingsImageAugmenter`` (optional crop_settings)
8	  * ``get_val_dataloader`` → WDS branch when ``use_wds: true`` (stock val is folder-only)
9	
10	Train uses stock ``get_train_dataloader`` → ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader`` unchanged.
11	Neural transforms are stock ``AbstractTransform`` subclasses registered in
12	``MODALITY_TRANSFORMS`` via ``fourm_neural_modalities``.
13	"""
14	
15	from __future__ import annotations
16	
17	import copy
18	from functools import partial
19	
20	import webdataset as wds
21	from fourm.data import pretrain_utils
22	from fourm.data import unified_datasets as ud
23	from fourm.data import image_augmenter as ia
24	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CropSettingsTransform, IdentityTransform
25	from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import cfgs_get
26	from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
27	    default_collate,
28	    filter_metadata,
29	    map,
30	    multi_tarfile_samples,
31	    remove_extensions,
32	    rename_modalities,
33	    tok_to_int64,
34	    wds_decoder,
35	)
36	import torchvision.transforms as transforms
37	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import UnifiedDataTransform
38	
39	import fourm_neural_modalities
40	from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
41	from things_augmenter import ThingsImageAugmenter
42	
43	_PRESENCE_PATHS = {"meg_mask": "meg_mask", "eeg_mask": "eeg_mask"}
44	
45	_ORIG_UNIFIED_MASKING = ud.UnifiedMasking
46	_ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG = ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter
47	_ORIG_GET_VAL = pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader
48	_ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES = ud.rename_modalities
49	_PATCHED = False
50	
51	
52	class _SeqSafeRandom:
53	    """Proxy for the stdlib ``random`` module that lists ``sample`` populations.
54	
55	    Stock 4M's decoder does ``random.sample(mod_dict.items(), …)``; ``random.sample``
56	    rejected dict views / sets starting in Python 3.11. Swapping ``fm.random`` for
57	    this proxy keeps the model forward working on 3.11+ without editing ``ml-4m`` —
58	    every other attribute delegates to the real module unchanged.
59	    """
60	
61	    def __init__(self, real):
62	        self._real = real
63	
64	    def sample(self, population, k):
65	        return self._real.sample(list(population), k)
66	
67	    def __getattr__(self, name):
68	        return getattr(self._real, name)
69	
70	
71	def _rename_modalities(sample, modality_paths):
72	    """Stock rename assumes every path exists; THINGS omits optional ``crop_settings`` tars."""
73	    present = {out: src for out, src in modality_paths.items() if src in sample}
74	    if not present:
75	        return sample
76	    return _ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES(sample, present)
77	
78	
79	def _extend_modality_paths(modality_info: dict) -> dict[str, str]:
80	    paths = {mod: modality_info[mod].get("path", None) or mod for mod in modality_info}
81	    paths.update(_PRESENCE_PATHS)
82	    return paths
83	
84	
85	def _wds_eval_loader(
86	    data_path: str,
87	    all_domains: list[str],
88	    modality_info: dict,
89	    modality_transforms: dict,
90	    image_augmenter,
91	    text_tokenizer,
92	    input_tokens_range,
93	    target_tokens_range,
94	    num_workers: int,
95	    batch_size: int,
96	    sampling_weights=None,
97	    modality_name_map=None,
98	):
99	    """Deterministic WDS val loader — only gap stock 4M does not cover.
100	
101	    Reuses the same transform stack as ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader``
102	    (``UnifiedDataTransform`` + patched ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking``).
103	    Pipeline differs only in shard source (``SimpleShardList``, no shuffle/repeat).
104	    """
105	    fourm_neural_modalities.register(training=False)
106	
107	    modality_paths = _extend_modality_paths(modality_info)
108	    modality_transforms = copy.deepcopy(modality_transforms)
109	    if any(modality_info[d].get("pretokenized", False) for d in all_domains):
110	        modality_transforms["crop_settings"] = CropSettingsTransform()
111	    modality_transforms["__key__"] = IdentityTransform()
112	
113	    transform = transforms.Compose(
114	        [
115	            UnifiedDataTransform(
116	                transforms_dict=modality_transforms,
117	                image_augmenter=image_augmenter,
118	            ),
119	            PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
120	                modality_info=modality_info,
121	                text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
122	                input_tokens_range=input_tokens_range,
123	                target_tokens_range=target_tokens_range,
124	                sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
125	            ),
126	        ]
127	    )
128	
129	    datapipe = wds.DataPipeline(
130	        wds.SimpleShardList(data_path),
131	        partial(multi_tarfile_samples, modality_name_map=modality_name_map),
132	        wds.decode(wds_decoder),
133	        wds.map(remove_extensions),
134	        map(filter_metadata),
135	        map(tok_to_int64),
136	        # Tolerant rename: a task's shards may omit optional folders (e.g. meg_mask
137	        # for a vision-only val task), so skip paths not present in the sample.
138	        map(partial(_rename_modalities, modality_paths=modality_paths)),
139	        map(transform),
140	        wds.batched(batch_size, collation_fn=default_collate, partial=False),
141	    )
142	    return wds.WebLoader(datapipe, num_workers=num_workers, batch_size=None)
143	
144	
145	def _neural_get_val_dataloader(
146	    dataset_config,
147	    dataset_name,
148	    train_configs,
149	    modality_info,
150	    sampling_weights,
151	    text_tokenizer,
152	    input_size,
153	    num_input_tokens,
154	    num_target_tokens,
155	    min_input_tokens,
156	    min_target_tokens,
157	    fixed_eval,
158	    fixed_eval_input_tokens,
159	    fixed_eval_target_tokens,
160	    dist_eval,
161	    num_tasks,
162	    num_workers,
163	    batch_size,
164	    pin_mem,
165	):
166	    """Stock val loader, plus WDS tars when ``use_wds: true`` in val config."""
167	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
168	    from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CaptionTransform
169	    from fourm.data.image_augmenter import CenterCropImageAugmenter

221:def rename_modalities(sample, modality_paths):
def rename_modalities(sample, modality_paths):
    """
    Renames modalities to their corresponding names in modality_paths.
    """
    return {out_path: sample[loaded_path] for out_path, loaded_path in modality_paths.items()}

Assistant2026-05-27T20:04:30.649Z

I now have a fully validated mechanism. Before writing code, here's the design and the system-level reasoning — then I'll implement it test-first.

Design: neural as additive, leak-free output modalities

Decision 1 — a custom modality type, not img and not seq_token. This is the load-bearing choice: - seq_token (current) routes targets through the autoregressive left-shift path at fm.py:309 — the documented "MEG loss = 0" bug. - img would route correctly (parallel), but the real trainer overwrites every img modality's max_tokens with (image_size/patch_size)² at run_training_4m.py:250 — always a perfect square. Our grids are 128 (16×8) and 17, not squares. Incompatible. - A new type string (neural_grid) falls through to the parallel decoder branch (fm.py:320) and is skipped by the square-max_tokens overwrite — so our max_tokens survives. I verified every training-path type branch in fourm/ is safe with an unknown type (encoder cat is type-agnostic; masking is our own subclass; empty-mod-dict falls to the correct 1-D else). No external/ml-4m edits.

Decision 2 — purely additive output modalities (don't touch the existing inputs). Rather than changing tok_meg/tok_eeg's type (which would churn the input-only design, val tasks, and H1/H5 tests), I add new decoder-only modalities that read the same folders via 4M's rename_modalities fan-out — no shard repack:

New modality type path (folder) grid vocab head
tok_meg_rvq0..3 neural_grid tok_meg 128 cells (16×8, axial pos) 512 4 separate heads
tok_eeg_out neural_grid tok_eeg 17 (1-D pos) 8192 1 head

The 4 MEG heads realize your §6 "4 logit heads, one per RVQ layer"; loss sums across them via forward_mod_loss.

Decision 3 — coherent trial split + leak-free arrangement. The 4 RVQ modalities must come from the same trial. Per-modality transforms each draw their own random trial → decoherence. Fix: do the trial pick once per sample in the _rename_modalities seam we already own, splitting into 4 layers. For a clean regularizer with no answer-leakage, the shipped config predicts neural from vision (in: rgb+depth → out: rgb+depth+meg_rvq*+eeg_out); neural is not an encoder input, so there's nothing to copy. I will not touch 4m_things_val_tasks.yaml.

Let me set up the work and start test-first.

Assistant2026-05-27T20:06:21.290Z
Thinking
Assistant2026-05-27T20:06:36.829Z

Good — that's the right thing to nail down before any code. Short answer: yes, it's structurally guaranteed, because the trial is sampled exactly once in the data loader and that one tensor becomes both the embedded input and the loss target. There is no second sampling between the forward pass and backprop. Let me trace it concretely so you can see why.

Where the trial is picked: once per sample, in the data-loading transform (CPU, in the DataLoader worker). The result is a single token array T for that modality in that batch element. The model never re-samples — T is frozen for the entire forward/backward step.

How T becomes the target. For a parallel (img / our neural_grid) modality, the decoder embedding's forward_embed does this (decoder_embeddings.py:242-254):

ids = d['tensor']          # <-- the sampled trial T
ids = ids.reshape(B, -1)
x   = self.token_emb(ids)
d['x']   = x
d['ids'] = ids             # <-- target ids ARE the same T

Then in cat_decoder_tensors (fm.py:322-323):

decoder_tokens_all.append(torch.zeros_like(d['x']) + self.mask_token)  # input = MASK, not T
target_ids_all.append(d['ids'])                                        # label  = T

and the loss (fm.py:597) is cross_entropy(logits, target_ids) over exactly those d['ids']. So:

  • The decoder input at a target position is the mask token (so there's no leakage — the model can't just copy the answer).
  • The label at that position is T — the very trial that was sampled.
  • They are the same array object, set in the same forward_embed call. Nothing can desync them.

The only desync risk is the one we engineered around: the 4 MEG RVQ layers are 4 separate modalities. If each ran its own trial-sampling transform, layer 0 might be trial 7 and layer 2 trial 3 — incoherent across heads. That's exactly why the plan picks the trial once in the shared _rename_modalities seam and slices all 4 layers from that single pick. Within each head, the "input-embedding vs. loss-target" coherence above is automatic; across heads, the single shared pick guarantees they describe the same MEG token.

One caveat to flag: this also means a modality used as both encoder input and decoder target must be the same modality name so one T is split (some cells visible, the rest predicted) by image_mask — leak-free. Our output-only-from-vision config sidesteps this entirely: neural cells are all targets, none are encoder inputs.

This is a genuinely subtle, reusable concept. Want me to write it up in notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md (extending §6) as a short "trial sampling ↔ loss-target coherence" section before I implement? And shall I re-run the baseline test collection (the pytest --co I just attempted) to confirm a green starting point?

38	def _ids(batch: int = 2) -> torch.Tensor:
39	    g = torch.Generator().manual_seed(1)
40	    return torch.randint(0, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (batch, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, MEG_N_RVQ), generator=g)

43	class TestShapeAndLifecycle:
44	    def test_lazy_init_then_forward(self):
45	        e = MegEncoderEmbedding()  # no dim yet
46	        with pytest.raises(AssertionError):
47	            e.forward({"tensor": _ids()})

54	class TestRvqSummation:
55	    def test_content_is_sum_of_per_layer_codebooks(self):
56	        e = _emb()
57	        ids = _ids()
58	        x = e.forward({"tensor": ids})["x"]
59	        expected = sum(e.codebooks[q](ids[..., q]) for q in range(MEG_N_RVQ))
60	        assert torch.allclose(x, expected, atol=1e-6)
61	
62	    def test_layers_use_distinct_codebooks(self):
63	        """Same code value in different RVQ layers must embed differently."""
64	        e = _emb()
65	        same = torch.zeros(1, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, MEG_N_RVQ, dtype=torch.long)
66	        same[..., 0] = 5  # code 5 only in layer 0
67	        only0 = e.forward({"tensor": same})["x"]
68	        same2 = torch.zeros_like(same)
69	        same2[..., 1] = 5  # code 5 only in layer 1
70	        only1 = e.forward({"tensor": same2})["x"]
71	        assert not torch.allclose(only0, only1), "layers 0 and 1 share a codebook"
72	
73	    def test_every_layer_contributes(self):
74	        e = _emb()
75	        base = torch.zeros(1, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, MEG_N_RVQ, dtype=torch.long)

77	        for q in range(MEG_N_RVQ):

79	            bumped[..., q] = 7

88	        emb = e.forward({"tensor": ids})["emb"][0]  # (P, D)
89	        # identical content everywhere -> any position difference is purely positional
90	        assert not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[1]), "adjacent cells share a position embedding"
91	
92	    def test_source_and_time_axes_both_matter(self):
93	        e = _emb()
94	        ids = torch.full((1, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, MEG_N_RVQ), 3, dtype=torch.long)
95	        emb = e.forward({"tensor": ids})["emb"][0]
96	        # cell p -> source=p//n_time, time=p%n_time
97	        same_source_diff_time = not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[1])          # (s0,t0) vs (s0,t1)
98	        same_time_diff_source = not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[MEG_N_TIME])  # (s0,t0) vs (s1,t0)
99	        assert same_source_diff_time and same_time_diff_source
100

# Data config for THINGS multimodal training (vision + MEG + EEG).
# data_path shards use braceexpand ranges, e.g. shard_{000..026}.tar → shard_000.tar … shard_026.tar
# (shard_{000}.tar alone is wrong — braces are not expanded and the file is missing).
#
# in_domains / out_domains (hyphen-separated):
#   Modalities that may appear on the encoder (input) vs decoder (target) side.
#   tok_meg / tok_eeg are INPUT-ONLY (encoder-only): put them in in_domains, never
#   out_domains (config_validate enforces this). Example — predict depth from
#   RGB + brain signals:
#     in_domains: tok_rgb-tok_depth-tok_meg-tok_eeg
#     out_domains: tok_depth
#   Keep meg_mask / eeg_mask out of these lists (presence flags only, not trained tokens).
#
# input_alphas / target_alphas (Dirichlet concentration, one value per in/out domain):
#   Control how the random input/target token budget is split across modalities each step.
#   Higher alpha → that modality gets a larger share of tokens more often.
#   Use 0.0 on an in_domain to rarely/never use it as input; 0.0 on out_domain to skip as target.
#   Single value "1.0" applies to all listed domains. For rgb→dense mixtures see upstream
#   cfgs/default/4m/alphas_mixture/ and set alphas_config instead of simple alphas.
#
# train.weights: relative sampling rate when multiple entries exist under train.datasets
#   (e.g. [0.8, 0.2] = 80% THINGS, 20% CC12M once cc12m is uncommented).

train:
  datasets:

1	"""4M-compatible AbstractTransform adapters for neural modalities."""
2	
3	from __future__ import annotations
4	
5	import numpy as np
6	import torch
7	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import AbstractTransform
8	
9	from neural_constants import EEG_CODE_MAX, MEG_CODE_MAX
10	from neural_trial_transform import (
11	    EegTrialSampleTransform,
12	    MegTrialSampleTransform,
13	)
14	
15	
16	class MegTokTransform(AbstractTransform):
17	    """Pick one MEG trial per call and return a (MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,) int64 tensor."""
18	
19	    def __init__(self, training: bool = True, seed: int | None = None):
20	        self.sampler = MegTrialSampleTransform(training=training, seed=seed)
21	
22	    def load(self, path: str) -> np.ndarray:
23	        return np.load(path, allow_pickle=False)
24	
25	    def preprocess(self, sample: np.ndarray) -> torch.Tensor:
26	        tokens, _valid = self.sampler(sample)
27	        tokens = np.clip(tokens, 0, MEG_CODE_MAX)
28	        return torch.from_numpy(tokens).long()
29	
30	    def image_augment(
31	        self,
32	        v,
33	        crop_coords,
34	        flip,
35	        orig_size,
36	        target_size,
37	        rand_aug_idx,
38	        resample_mode=None,
39	    ):
40	        return v
41	
42	    def postprocess(self, sample):
43	        return sample
44	
45	
46	class EegTokTransform(AbstractTransform):
47	    """Pick one EEG trial per call and return a (EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,) int64 tensor."""
48	
49	    def __init__(self, training: bool = True, seed: int | None = None):
50	        self.sampler = EegTrialSampleTransform(training=training, seed=seed)
51	
52	    def load(self, path: str) -> np.ndarray:
53	        return np.load(path, allow_pickle=False)
54	
55	    def preprocess(self, sample: np.ndarray) -> torch.Tensor:
56	        tokens, _valid = self.sampler(sample)
57	        tokens = np.clip(tokens, 0, EEG_CODE_MAX)
58	        return torch.from_numpy(tokens).long()
59	
60	    def image_augment(self, v, *args, **kwargs):
61	        return v
62	
63	    def postprocess(self, sample):
64	        return sample
65	
66	
67	class MaskFlagTransform(AbstractTransform):
68	    """Pass-through for uint8 presence flags (``meg_mask`` / ``eeg_mask``)."""
69	
70	    def load(self, path: str) -> np.ndarray:
71	        return np.load(path, allow_pickle=False)
72	
73	    def preprocess(self, sample: np.ndarray) -> torch.Tensor:
74	        return torch.from_numpy(sample.astype(np.int64))
75	
76	    def image_augment(self, v, *args, **kwargs):
77	        return v
78	
79	    def postprocess(self, sample):
80	        return sample

Tool reply2026-05-27T20:18:38.812Z
1	"""Overfit-one-batch sanity check — the minimum bar before any real training.
2	
3	A model that cannot drive the loss down on a single fixed batch has a broken
4	forward/backward path, and no amount of data or compute will fix that. This
5	harness builds ``fm_tiny``, takes ONE batch with every modality present, and
6	runs a handful of optimizer steps on that same batch. If wiring is correct,
7	*each* modality's loss falls monotonically toward zero.
8	
9	This is not training — it is a unit-level "does gradient flow to every head"
10	test. Runs on CPU in seconds; also exposed as a Modal entrypoint for GPU.
11	"""
12	
13	from __future__ import annotations
14	
15	import sys
16	from pathlib import Path
17	
18	import numpy as np
19	import torch
20	
21	# Library modules live in lib/; put it on sys.path so the flat imports below resolve.
22	sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "lib"))
23	
24	from repo_paths import TEXT_TOKENIZER  # noqa: E402
25	
26	import fourm_neural_modalities  # noqa: F401,E402 — register modalities + transforms
27	from fourm_dataloader import patch_pretrain_utils  # noqa: E402
28	from neural_constants import (  # noqa: E402
29	    EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
30	    EEG_VOCAB_SIZE,
31	    MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
32	    MEG_VOCAB_SIZE,
33	    THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
34	    TOK_DEPTH_VOCAB_SIZE,
35	    TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,
36	    TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE,
37	)
38	
39	patch_pretrain_utils()
40	
41	# Neural mods are input-only: encoded but never predicted. Vision tokens are the
42	# targets whose loss must descend. See notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md.
43	_IN_DOMAINS = ["tok_rgb", "tok_depth", "tok_meg", "tok_eeg"]
44	_OUT_DOMAINS = ["tok_rgb", "tok_depth"]
45	
46	
47	def _decoded_sample(rng: np.random.Generator) -> dict:
48	    """One image with every modality present (mask=1) and in-vocab tokens."""
49	    return {
50	        "tok_rgb": rng.integers(0, TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE, (TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,)).astype(np.int64),
51	        "tok_depth": rng.integers(0, TOK_DEPTH_VOCAB_SIZE, (TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,)).astype(np.int64),
52	        "tok_meg": rng.integers(0, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (2, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)).astype(np.int64),

📝 Write test_neural_output_modalities.py
/Users/Siddharth/neural-foundation-model/4m_training/tests/test_neural_output_modalities.py
"""Contract + integration tests for neural (MEG/EEG) OUTPUT modalities.

These lock the design in notes/4m_neural_modality_design.md §6 as realized:

  * MEG is predicted with 4 parallel heads (one per RVQ layer) — registered as
    4 ``neural_grid`` modalities ``tok_meg_rvq0..3`` (vocab 512, 128-cell grid).
  * EEG is predicted with one head — ``tok_eeg_out`` (vocab 8192, 17 tokens).
  * The output modalities use a custom ``neural_grid`` type so they route through
    the *parallel* decoder branch (not the autoregressive seq_token path) and are
    *not* clobbered by the trainer's square ``max_tokens`` rule for ``img``.
  * The 4 MEG heads come from the SAME sampled trial (coherent split).
  * The existing input-only ``tok_meg`` / ``tok_eeg`` modalities are untouched.

Fast + CPU-only.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import sys
from pathlib import Path

import numpy as np
import pytest
import torch

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parent))

import fourm_neural_modalities  # noqa: F401 — registers modalities at import
from fourm_neural_embeddings import EegDecoderEmbedding, MegRVQDecoderEmbedding
from neural_constants import (
    EEG_OUT_MODALITY,
    EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,
    EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
    EEG_VOCAB_SIZE,
    MEG_GRID_SHAPE,
    MEG_N_RVQ,
    MEG_N_SOURCES,
    MEG_N_TIME,
    MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL,
    MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES,
    MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
    MEG_VOCAB_SIZE,
    NEURAL_GRID_TYPE,
)

_DIM = 32


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Decoder embeddings (parallel heads)
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestMegRVQDecoderEmbedding:
    def _emb(self) -> MegRVQDecoderEmbedding:
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        e = MegRVQDecoderEmbedding(vocab_size=MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, n_sources=MEG_N_SOURCES, n_time=MEG_N_TIME)
        e.init(dim_tokens=_DIM)
        return e.eval()

    def _ids(self, batch: int = 2) -> torch.Tensor:
        g = torch.Generator().manual_seed(1)
        return torch.randint(0, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (batch, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL), generator=g)

    def test_forward_embed_shapes(self):
        e = self._emb()
        out = e.forward_embed({"tensor": self._ids()})
        assert out["x"].shape == (2, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, _DIM)
        assert out["emb"].shape == (2, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, _DIM)
        assert out["ids"].shape == (2, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL)

    def test_forward_logits_maps_to_vocab(self):
        e = self._emb()
        y = torch.randn(7, _DIM)  # 7 selected decoder tokens
        logits = e.forward_logits(y)
        assert logits.shape == (7, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE)

    def test_axial_positions_source_and_time_both_matter(self):
        e = self._emb()
        ids = torch.full((1, MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL), 3, dtype=torch.long)
        emb = e.forward_embed({"tensor": ids})["emb"][0]  # (P, D), content identical
        same_source_diff_time = not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[1])          # (s0,t0) vs (s0,t1)
        same_time_diff_source = not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[MEG_N_TIME])  # (s0,t0) vs (s1,t0)
        assert same_source_diff_time and same_time_diff_source

    def test_lazy_init_required_before_forward(self):
        e = MegRVQDecoderEmbedding()
        with pytest.raises(AssertionError):
            e.forward_embed({"tensor": self._ids()})

    def test_accepts_share_embedding_kwarg(self):
        # The HF FM wrapper passes share_embedding=False to non-img decoder factories.
        MegRVQDecoderEmbedding(vocab_size=MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, share_embedding=False)


class TestEegDecoderEmbedding:
    def _emb(self) -> EegDecoderEmbedding:
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        e = EegDecoderEmbedding(vocab_size=EEG_VOCAB_SIZE, max_length=EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL)
        e.init(dim_tokens=_DIM)
        return e.eval()

    def test_forward_embed_shapes(self):
        e = self._emb()
        ids = torch.randint(0, EEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (2, EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL))
        out = e.forward_embed({"tensor": ids})
        assert out["x"].shape == (2, EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL, _DIM)
        assert out["emb"].shape == (2, EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL, _DIM)
        assert out["ids"].shape == (2, EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL)

    def test_forward_logits_maps_to_vocab(self):
        e = self._emb()
        logits = e.forward_logits(torch.randn(5, _DIM))
        assert logits.shape == (5, EEG_VOCAB_SIZE)

    def test_positions_vary_along_sequence(self):
        e = self._emb()
        ids = torch.full((1, EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL), 4, dtype=torch.long)
        emb = e.forward_embed({"tensor": ids})["emb"][0]
        assert not torch.allclose(emb[0], emb[1])


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Modality registration
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestRegistration:
    def _info(self):
        from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO

        return MODALITY_INFO

    def test_four_meg_rvq_modalities_registered(self):
        info = self._info()
        assert len(MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES) == MEG_N_RVQ
        for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES:
            assert mod in info, mod
            m = info[mod]
            assert m["type"] == NEURAL_GRID_TYPE
            assert m["vocab_size"] == MEG_VOCAB_SIZE
            assert m["max_tokens"] == MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL
            assert m["path"] == "tok_meg"           # reads the same on-disk folder
            assert m.get("encoder_embedding") is None  # output-only
            assert m.get("decoder_embedding") is not None
            assert m.get("pretokenized") is True

    def test_eeg_out_modality_registered(self):
        m = self._info()[EEG_OUT_MODALITY]
        assert m["type"] == NEURAL_GRID_TYPE
        assert m["vocab_size"] == EEG_VOCAB_SIZE
        assert m["max_tokens"] == EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL
        assert m["path"] == "tok_eeg"
        assert m.get("encoder_embedding") is None
        assert m.get("decoder_embedding") is not None

    def test_input_only_neural_modalities_unchanged(self):
        info = self._info()
        # The original input-only modalities must keep no decoder head.
        assert info["tok_meg"].get("decoder_embedding") is None
        assert info["tok_eeg"].get("decoder_embedding") is None

    def test_transforms_registered_for_output_modalities(self):
        from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS

        for mod in (*MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES, EEG_OUT_MODALITY):
            assert mod in MODALITY_TRANSFORMS, mod


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Coherent trial split (the 4 MEG heads share one trial)
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestCoherentTrialSplit:
    def _arr_per_trial_constant(self, n_trials: int = 5) -> np.ndarray:
        """arr[t] is entirely the constant (t+1) so we can identify the picked trial."""
        arr = np.zeros((n_trials, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), dtype=np.int16)
        for t in range(n_trials):
            arr[t] = t + 1
        return arr

    def test_all_four_meg_layers_from_same_trial(self):
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter

        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=True, seed=0)
        arr = self._arr_per_trial_constant()
        # rename aliases all four rvq keys to the same source array object.
        sample = {mod: arr for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES}
        splitter(sample)

        layers = [sample[mod] for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES]
        for layer in layers:
            assert layer.shape == (MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL,)
        # Every layer is a single constant (one trial) and they all agree.
        constants = {int(np.unique(layer)[0]) for layer in layers}
        assert len(constants) == 1, f"layers came from different trials: {constants}"

    def test_eval_mode_picks_first_trial(self):
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter

        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=False)
        arr = self._arr_per_trial_constant()
        sample = {mod: arr for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES}
        splitter(sample)
        assert int(np.unique(sample[MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES[0]])[0]) == 1  # trial 0 -> constant 1

    def test_eeg_out_split_single_trial(self):
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter

        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=False)
        arr = np.stack([np.full(EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE, t + 1, dtype=np.int16) for t in range(3)])
        sample = {EEG_OUT_MODALITY: arr}
        splitter(sample)
        assert sample[EEG_OUT_MODALITY].shape == (EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,)
        assert int(np.unique(sample[EEG_OUT_MODALITY])[0]) == 1

    def test_sentinel_meg_becomes_placeholder(self):
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter

        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=True, seed=0)
        sentinel = np.full((1, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
        sample = {mod: sentinel for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES}
        splitter(sample)
        for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES:
            assert sample[mod].shape == (MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL,)
            assert (sample[mod] >= 0).all()  # sentinel -1 clipped to placeholder 0

    def test_split_is_noop_without_neural_keys(self):
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter

        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=True, seed=0)
        sample = {"tok_rgb": np.zeros((196,), dtype=np.int64)}
        splitter(sample)
        assert set(sample) == {"tok_rgb"}


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Masking: neural_grid routes through the parallel image_mask path
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestNeuralGridMasking:
    @pytest.fixture
    def masking(self):
        from tokenizers import Tokenizer

        from repo_paths import REPO_ROOT
        from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking

        tok = Tokenizer.from_file(
            str(
                REPO_ROOT
                / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/"
                "text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"
            )
        )
        modality_info = {
            "tok_rgb": {
                "type": "seq_token", "min_tokens": 0, "max_tokens": 196,
                "input_alphas": [1.0], "target_alphas": [1.0], "vocab_offset": 0,
            },
            "tok_meg_rvq0": {
                "type": NEURAL_GRID_TYPE, "min_tokens": 0,
                "max_tokens": MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL,
                "input_alphas": [0.0], "target_alphas": [1.0],
            },
        }
        return PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
            modality_info=modality_info, text_tokenizer=tok,
            input_tokens_range=(64, 64), target_tokens_range=(64, 64),
        )

    def test_present_output_has_targets_and_no_sentinel_ids(self, masking):
        out = masking({
            "tok_rgb": torch.arange(196, dtype=torch.long),
            "tok_meg_rvq0": torch.randint(0, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL,)),
            "meg_mask": torch.tensor([1]),
        })
        meg = out["tok_meg_rvq0"]
        assert (~meg["target_mask"]).sum() > 0                 # produces decoder targets
        assert int(meg["tensor"].max()) < MEG_VOCAB_SIZE       # no text-sentinel injection
        assert int(meg["tensor"].min()) >= 0
        assert meg["tensor"].shape[0] == MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL  # parallel grid, not span-padded

    def test_absent_output_zeroed_via_presence_flag(self, masking):
        out = masking({
            "tok_rgb": torch.arange(196, dtype=torch.long),
            "tok_meg_rvq0": torch.zeros(MEG_POSITIONS_PER_TRIAL, dtype=torch.long),
            "meg_mask": torch.tensor([0]),
        })
        assert (~out["tok_meg_rvq0"]["target_mask"]).sum() == 0

class TestConfigValidation:

            "in_domains": "tok_rgb",
            "out_domains": "-".join(["tok_rgb", *MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES, EEG_OUT_MODALITY]),
            "main_augment_domain": "tok_rgb",
            "input_alphas": "1.0",
            "target_alphas": "1.0",

        from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO

        from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO

        errors = validate_dataset_config("things", ds, REPO_ROOT, MODALITY_INFO)
        assert any("tok_meg_rvq0" in e for e in errors)


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Integration: neural heads produce a finite loss and receive gradient
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


class TestNeuralOutputGradientFlow:
    def _batch_and_model(self):
        from tokenizers import Tokenizer

        from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
        from fourm.data.modality_transforms import IdentityTransform, UnifiedDataTransform
        from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import setup_sampling_mod_info
        from fourm.data.unified_datasets import default_collate
        from fourm.utils import create_model

        from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
        from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter
        from repo_paths import TEXT_TOKENIZER
        from things_augmenter import ThingsImageAugmenter
        from train_4m import _build_modality_info
        from neural_constants import THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE, TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE, TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE

        in_domains = ["tok_rgb"]
        out_domains = ["tok_rgb", *MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES, EEG_OUT_MODALITY]
        all_d = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
        full = _build_modality_info(all_d, input_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)

        ds_cfg = {
            "in_domains": "-".join(sorted(in_domains)),
            "out_domains": "-".join(sorted(out_domains)),
            "input_alphas": "-".join("1.0" for _ in in_domains),
            "target_alphas": "-".join("1.0" for _ in out_domains),
        }
        mask_info, _ = setup_sampling_mod_info(ds_cfg, full)

        text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(str(TEXT_TOKENIZER))
        transforms = dict(MODALITY_TRANSFORMS)
        transforms["__key__"] = IdentityTransform()
        udt = UnifiedDataTransform(
            transforms_dict=transforms,
            image_augmenter=ThingsImageAugmenter(
                target_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE, no_aug=True, main_domain="tok_rgb"
            ),
        )
        splitter = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=True, seed=0)

        def decoded(rng):
            arr_meg = rng.integers(0, MEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (3, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)).astype(np.int16)
            arr_eeg = rng.integers(0, EEG_VOCAB_SIZE, (3, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)).astype(np.int16)
            sample = {
                "tok_rgb": rng.integers(0, TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE, (TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,)).astype(np.int64),
                "meg_mask": np.array([1], dtype=np.int64),
                "eeg_mask": np.array([1], dtype=np.int64),
                "__key__": "x",
            }
            # rename fan-out: all 4 rvq keys alias the MEG source; eeg_out aliases EEG source.
            for mod in MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES:
                sample[mod] = arr_meg
            sample[EEG_OUT_MODALITY] = arr_eeg
            splitter(sample)
            return sample

        # Build a batch where every neural head has at least one target.
        for attempt in range(50):
            torch.manual_seed(attempt)
            masker = PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
                modality_info=mask_info, text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
                input_tokens_range=(96, 96), target_tokens_range=(96, 96),
            )
            rng = np.random.default_rng(attempt)
            samples = [masker(udt(decoded(rng))) for _ in range(2)]
            batch = default_collate(samples)
            neural = [*MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES, EEG_OUT_MODALITY]
            if all(int((~batch[m]["target_mask"]).sum()) > 0 for m in neural):
                break
        else:
            pytest.skip("could not assemble a batch with all neural targets present")

        enc = {m: full[m]["encoder_embedding"](patch_size=full[m].get("patch_size", 16),
                                               image_size=THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
               if full[m]["type"] == "img" else full[m]["encoder_embedding"]()
               for m in in_domains}
        dec = {m: full[m]["decoder_embedding"]() for m in out_domains}
        model = create_model(
            "fm_tiny_6e_6d_swiglu_nobias", encoder_embeddings=enc, decoder_embeddings=dec,
            modality_info=full, num_register_tokens=0,
        )
        return model, batch, [*MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES, EEG_OUT_MODALITY]

    def test_loss_finite_and_gradient_reaches_meg_head(self):
        from fourm_dataloader import patch_pretrain_utils

        patch_pretrain_utils()
        model, batch, neural = self._batch_and_model()
        model.train()
        loss, mod_loss = model(batch, loss_type="mod")
        assert torch.isfinite(loss)
        for m in neural:
            assert m in mod_loss and torch.isfinite(mod_loss[m]).all()
            assert float(mod_loss[m]) > 0
        loss.backward()
        head = model.decoder_embeddings[MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES[0]].to_logits.weight
        assert head.grad is not None and head.grad.abs().sum() > 0

EEG_VOCAB_SIZE: int = 8192
EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE: tuple[int] = (17,)

# --- Neural OUTPUT (target) modalities ---
# MEG/EEG can be predicted as a reconstruction regularizer (see notes §6). They use a
# custom modality ``type`` so 4M routes them through the PARALLEL decoder branch
# (fm.py cat_decoder_tensors) rather than the autoregressive seq_token path, and so the
# trainer's square ``max_tokens`` rule for ``img`` (run_training_4m.setup_modality_info)
# leaves their non-square grids (128, 17) untouched.
NEURAL_GRID_TYPE: str = "neural_grid"
# One target head per RVQ layer (layer-specific 512-vocab codebooks): 4 modalities, each a
# 128-cell (16x8) grid of single codes. All read the on-disk ``tok_meg`` folder.
MEG_RVQ_OUT_MODALITIES: tuple[str, ...] = tuple(f"tok_meg_rvq{q}" for q in range(MEG_N_RVQ))
MEG_OUT_SOURCE_PATH: str = "tok_meg"
# EEG is a single codebook -> one head over its 17-token sequence; reads ``tok_eeg`` folder.
EEG_OUT_MODALITY: str = "tok_eeg_out"
EEG_OUT_SOURCE_PATH: str = "tok_eeg"

def build_1d_sincos_posemb(max_len, embed_dim=1024, temperature=10000.):
    """Sine-cosine positional embeddings from MoCo-v3, adapted back to 1d

    Returns positional embedding of shape (1, N, D)
    """
    arange = torch.arange(max_len, dtype=torch.float32) # Shape (N,)
    assert embed_dim % 2 == 0, 'Embed dimension must be divisible by 2 for 1D sin-cos position embedding'
    pos_dim = embed_dim // 2
    omega = torch.arange(pos_dim, dtype=torch.float32) / pos_dim # Shape (D/2,)
    omega = 1. / (temperature ** omega)
    out = torch.einsum('n,d->nd', [arange, omega]) # Outer product, shape (N, D/2)
    pos_emb = torch.cat([torch.sin(out), torch.cos(out)], dim=1).unsqueeze(0) # Shape (1, N, D)
    return pos_emb
